    window.loadScript = (url, { charset = 'UTF-8', ...attributes } = {}, location = 'head') => {
      const existingScript = document.querySelector('script[src="' + url + '"]');
      if (existingScript) {
        return;
      }

      const script = document.createElement('script');
      script.src = url;
      script.type = 'text/javascript';

      script.async = true;
      script.charset = charset;

      if (attributes) {
        Object.entries(attributes).forEach(([key, value]) => {
          script.setAttribute(key, value);
        });
      }

      if (location === 'head') {
        document.head.appendChild(script);
      } else {
        document.body.appendChild(script);
      }

      return script;
    };

humans&quot;],&quot;canonical&quot;:[0,&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/account-abuse-protection&quot;],&quot;info&quot;:[0,{&quot;id&quot;:[0,&quot;3oZLDQYiufcZZYvGXwxpKd&quot;],&quot;title&quot;:[0,&quot;Announcing isnГўВҖВҷt enough anymore. CloudflareГўВҖВҷs new fraud prevention capabilities ГўВҖВ” now available in Early Access ГўВҖВ” help stop account abuse before it starts.&quot;],&quot;featured&quot;:[0,false],&quot;html&quot;:[0,&quot;&lt;p&gt;Today, Cloudflare is introducing a new suite of fraud prevention capabilities designed to stop account abuse before it starts. We&amp;#39;ve spent years empowering Cloudflare customers to protect their applications from automated attacks, but the threat landscape has evolved. The industrialization of hybrid automated-and-human abuse presents a complex security challenge to website owners. Consider, for instance, a single account thatГўВҖВҷs accessed from New York, London, and San Francisco in the same five minutes. The core question in this case is not ГўВҖВңIs this automated?ГўВҖВқ but rather ГўВҖВңIs this authentic?ГўВҖВқГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Website owners need the tools to stop abuse on their website, no matter who itГўВҖВҷs coming from&lt;/b&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;During our Birthday Week in 2024, we gifted &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/detections/leaked-credentials/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;leaked credentials detection&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; to all customers, including everyone on a Free plan. Since then, we&amp;#39;ve added &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/bots/additional-configurations/detection-ids/#account-takeover-detections\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;account takeover detection IDs&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; as part of our &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/application-services/products/bot-management/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;bot management solution&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; to help identify bots attacking your login pages.ГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Now, weГўВҖВҷre combining these powerful tools with new ones. &lt;b&gt;Disposable email check&lt;/b&gt; and &lt;b&gt;email risk &lt;/b&gt;help you enforce security preferences for users who sign up with throwaway email addresses, a common tactic for fake account creation and promotion abuse, or whose emails are deemed risky based on email patterns and infrastructure. WeГўВҖВҷre also thrilled to introduce &lt;b&gt;Hashed User IDs&lt;/b&gt; ГўВҖВ” per-domain identifiers generated by cryptographically hashing usernames ГўВҖВ” that give customers better insight into suspicious account activity and greater ability to mitigate potentially fraudulent traffic, without compromising end user privacy.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;The new capabilities weГўВҖВҷre announcing today go beyond automation, identifying abusive behavior and risky identities among human users &lt;/b&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;i&gt;and&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;b&gt; bots. &lt;/b&gt;&lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/bots/account-abuse-protection/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Account Abuse Protection&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; is available in Early Access, and any Bot Management Enterprise customer can use these features at no additional cost for a limited period, until the general availability of Cloudflare Fraud Prevention later this year. If you want to learn more about this Early Access capability, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/lp/account-abuse-protection/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;sign up here&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h3 id=\&quot;leaked-credentials-make-logins-all-too-vulnerable\&quot;&gt;Leaked credentials make logins all too vulnerable&lt;/h3&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#leaked-credentials-make-logins-all-too-vulnerable\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;The barrier to entry for fraudulent behavior is dangerously low, especially with the availability of massive datasets and access to automated tools that commit account fraud at scale. Website owners arenГўВҖВҷt just dealing with individual hackers, but industrialized fraud. Last year, we highlighted how &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/password-reuse-rampant-half-user-logins-compromised/\&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;41% of logins across our network use leaked credentials&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. This number has only grown following the exposure of a database holding &lt;a href=\&quot;https://cybernews.com/security/billions-credentials-exposed-infostealers-data-leak/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;16 billion records&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, and multiple high-profile breaches have since come to light.ГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;WhatГўВҖВҷs more, users reuse passwords across multiple platforms, meaning a single leak from years ago can still unlock a high-value retail or even a bank account today. Our &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/detections/leaked-credentials/#leaked-credentials-fields\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;leaked credential check&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; is a free feature that checks whether a password has been leaked in a known data breach of another service or application on the Internet. This is a privacy-preserving credential checking service that helps protect our users from compromised credentials, meaning Cloudflare performs these checks without accessing or storing plaintext end user passwords. &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/helping-keep-customers-safe-with-leaked-password-notification/#how-does-cloudflare-check-for-leaked-credentials\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Passwords are hashed ГўВҖВ” i.e., converted into a random string of characters using a cryptographic algorithm ГўВҖВ” for the purpose of comparing them against a database of leaked credentials.&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; If you havenГўВҖВҷt already turned on our &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/detections/leaked-credentials/#leaked-credentials-fields\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;leaked credential check&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, enable it now to keep your accounts safe from easy hacks!&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Access to a large database of leaked credentials is only useful if an attacker can cycle through them quickly across many sites to identify which accounts are still vulnerable due to password reuse. In our Black Friday analysis in 2024, we observed that more than &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/grinch-bot-2024/\&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;60% of traffic to login pages across our network was automated&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. ThatГўВҖВҷs a lot of bots trying to break in.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;To help customers protect their login endpoints from constant bombardment, we added &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/learning/access-management/account-takeover/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;account takeover&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/bots/additional-configurations/detection-ids/account-takeover-detections/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;(ATO)-specific detections&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; to highlight suspicious traffic patterns. This is part of our recent focus on &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/per-customer-bot-defenses/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;per-customer detections&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, in which we provide behavioral anomaly detection unique to each bot management customer. Today, bot management customers can see and mitigate attempted ATO attacks in their login requests directly on the Security analytics dashboard.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/3f2nQ5wBVQ2WqiKGsjVWJe/3c1011ced84e46f65938f32c88035de9/image5.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1334\&quot; height=\&quot;492\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;In the card on the left within the Security analytics dashboard, you can view and address attempted account takeover attacks.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;In the last week, our ATO detections combined caught an average of &lt;b&gt;6.9 billion suspicious login attempts&lt;/b&gt; daily, across our network. These ATO detections, along with the many other detection mechanisms in our bot management solution, create a &lt;i&gt;layered defense&lt;/i&gt; against ATO and other malicious automated attacks.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h3 id=\&quot;from-automation-to-intent-and-identity\&quot;&gt;From automation to intent and identity&lt;/h3&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#from-automation-to-intent-and-identity\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;To discern automation, or to discern intent and identity? That is the question. Our answer: yes and yes, as both are critical layers of a robust security posture. Attackers now operate at a scale previously reserved for enterprise services: they leverage massive credential leaks, use human-powered fraud farms to spoof devices and locations, and create synthetic identities to maintain thousands ГўВҖВ” even millions ГўВҖВ” of fake accounts for promotion and platform abuse. A human being with automated tools could be draining accounts, abusing promotions, committing payment fraud, or all of the above.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Beyond that, automation is accessible like never before, particularly as users become better acquainted with using &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/learning/ai/what-is-agentic-ai/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;AI agents&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; and even long-standing, ГўВҖВңtraditionalГўВҖВқ browsers move toward having agentic capabilities by default. Whether itГўВҖВҷs a lone actor using an AI agent or a coordinated fraud campaign, the threat isnГўВҖВҷt as simple as a single script ГўВҖВ” it can involve human intent, with automated execution.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Consider the following scenarios weГўВҖВҷve heard from our customers:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;We have 1,000 new users this month, but more than half of them are fake identities who benefit from a free trial, then disappear.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;The attacker logged in with the correct password, so how do I know that it isnГўВҖВҷt the real user?&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;This entity is acting at human pace, and they are draining accounts.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;These problems can&amp;#39;t be solved by &lt;i&gt;only&lt;/i&gt; assessing automation; they require checking for authenticity and integrity. This is the gap that our dedicated fraud prevention capabilities address.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h3 id=\&quot;assessing-suspicious-emails\&quot;&gt;Assessing suspicious emails&lt;/h3&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#assessing-suspicious-emails\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;LetГўВҖВҷs start by assessing the earliest point of potential account abuse: account creation. Fake or bulk account creation is one of the biggest topics in conversations about website fraud, as it can open the door for attackers to access an application ГўВҖВ” or even an entire business model.ГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Cloudflare is giving customers the tools to assess suspicious account creation at the source in two ways:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Disposable email check&lt;/b&gt;: Detect when users sign up with disposable, or throwaway, email addresses commonly used for promotion abuse and fake account creation. These disposable email services allow attackers to spin up thousands of &amp;quot;unique&amp;quot; accounts without maintaining real infrastructure, particularly unauthenticated disposable emails that provide instant access without account creation or free unlimited email aliases. Customers can use this binary field as they build rules to enforce security preferences, choosing to block all disposable emails outright, or perhaps issuing a &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/cloudflare-challenges/challenge-types/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;challenge&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; to anyone attempting to create an account with a disposable email.\n&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/3PQC7PqKWrhl5c4OCXu5Ha/9340e3b49cc396ca5f5d01d34fd529d5/image2.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1638\&quot; height=\&quot;344\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Email risk:&lt;/b&gt; Cloudflare analyzes email patterns and infrastructure to provide risk tiers (low, medium, high) that customers can use in security rules. We know that not all email addresses are created equal; an address with the format &lt;code&gt;firstname.lastname@knowndomain.com&lt;/code&gt; carries different risk characteristics than &lt;code&gt;xk7q9m2p@newdomain.xyz&lt;/code&gt;. Email risk tiers allow customers to express their tolerance for risk and friction at the point of account creation.ГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;p&gt;Both disposable email check and email risk are now available in security analytics and security rules, equipping website owners to protect their account creation flow. These detections address a fundamental problem: by the time an account is committing abuse, it&amp;#39;s already too late. The website owner has already paid acquisition costs, the fraudulent user has consumed promotional credits, and remediation requires manual review. Mitigating suspicious emails means adding the appropriate friction at signup ГўВҖВ” the moment it matters most.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h3 id=\&quot;introducing-hashed-user-ids\&quot;&gt;Introducing Hashed User IDs&lt;/h3&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#introducing-hashed-user-ids\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;Understanding patterns of abuse requires &lt;i&gt;visibility&lt;/i&gt;: not only into the network, but of account activity. Traditionally, security has meant looking through the lens of IPs and isolated HTTP requests to spot automated activity, but website owners arenГўВҖВҷt just thinking in terms of network signals; they are also considering their users and known accounts. ThatГўВҖВҷs why weГўВҖВҷre expanding our mitigation toolbox to match the way applications are actually structured, focusing on user-based detection of fraudulent activity.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Attackers can effortlessly rotate IPs to hide their tracks. But forcing them to repeatedly generate new, credible accounts introduces massive friction, especially when combined with account creation protections. When we look past the network layer and map fraudulent actions to a given compromised or abusive account, we can spot targeted behavior tied to a single, persistent actor and put a stop to the abuse. In this way, weГўВҖВҷre shifting the defense strategy to the account level, instead of playing whack-a-mole with rotating IP addresses and residential proxies. This means that &lt;b&gt;our customers can mitigate abusive behavior based on the way &lt;/b&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;i&gt;their&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;b&gt; applications separate identity&lt;/b&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;To arm website owners with this capability, Cloudflare is releasing a &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/bots/account-abuse-protection/#user-id\&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Hashed User ID&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt; that customers can use in &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/analytics/security-analytics/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Security analytics&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/custom-rules/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Security rules&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, and &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/rules/transform/managed-transforms/reference/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Managed Transforms&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. User IDs are per-domain, cryptographically hashed versions of the values in the username field, and each user ID is an encrypted, unique, and stable identifier generated for a given username on a customer application. &lt;b&gt;Importantly, the actual username is not logged or stored by Cloudflare as part of this service.&lt;/b&gt; As with leaked credentials check and ATO detections, which identify login traffic and then encrypt credentials for comparison, we are prioritizing end user privacy while empowering our customers to take action against fraudulent behavior.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;With access to Hashed User IDs, website owners can:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;See top users: Which accounts have the most activity?&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;See when a unique user logs in from a country they usually donГўВҖВҷt ГўВҖВ” or multiple countries in one day!&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;Mitigate traffic based on unique user, such as blocking a user with historically suspicious activity.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;Combine fields to see when accounts are being targeted with leaked credentials.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;See what network patterns or signals are associated with unique users.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/3f7Jm4HnngjYEmKG8QSiyC/2ae3543f0cd0eb072a0c4c2bb12c4436/image4.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1110\&quot; height=\&quot;736\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;The expanded view of a single Hashed User ID within the Security analytics dashboard, showing the activity details of that unique user, including their login location and their browser.ГӮВ &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;This user-level visibility transforms how website owners can investigate and mitigate traffic. Instead of examining individual requests in isolation, our customers can see the full picture of how attackers are targeting and hiding among legitimate users.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h3 id=\&quot;take-the-next-step-in-account-protection-today\&quot;&gt;Take the next step in account protection today&lt;/h3&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#take-the-next-step-in-account-protection-today\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;If you want to learn more about this Early Access capability, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/lp/account-abuse-protection/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;sign up here&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. All Bot Management Enterprise customers are eligible to add these new Account Abuse Protection features today, and weГўВҖВҷd love to open the conversation with any and all &lt;a href=\&quot;http://www.cloudflare.com/lp/account-abuse-protection\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;prospective Bot Management customers&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;While bot detections will continue to answer the question of automation and intent, fraud detections delve into the question of authenticity. Together, they give website owners comprehensive tools to fight against the full spectrum of account abuse. This suite is one step in our ongoing investment to protect the entire user journey ГўВҖВ” from account creation and login to secure checkouts and the integrity of every interaction.&lt;/p&gt;&quot;],&quot;published_at&quot;:[0,&quot;2026-03-12T13:00+08:00&quot;],&quot;updated_at&quot;:[0,&quot;2026-03-12T13:00:12.058Z&quot;],&quot;feature_image&quot;:[0,&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/1xUHwg1io7QsO9sswX7GpD/2066c94abed41c9b6e4397173955cae7/image3.png&quot;],&quot;tags&quot;:[1,[[0,{&quot;id&quot;:[0,&quot;5tL3rXMWKG616Xmbnao9Oh&quot;],&quot;name&quot;:[0,&quot;Fraud&quot;],&quot;slug&quot;:[0,&quot;fraud&quot;]}],[0,{&quot;id&quot;:[0,&quot;6Mp7ouACN2rT3YjL1xaXJx&quot;],&quot;name&quot;:[0,&quot;Security&quot;],&quot;slug&quot;:[0,&quot;security&quot;]}]]],&quot;relatedTags&quot;:[0],&quot;authors&quot;:[1,[[0,{&quot;name&quot;:[0,&quot;Jin-Hee Lee&quot;],&quot;slug&quot;:[0,&quot;jin-hee-lee&quot;],&quot;bio&quot;:[0,null],&quot;profile_image&quot;:[0,&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/47LTVC3FaSVzkAumTWfFIi/4424dfc2819cbc4a8fff6b72ce93047e/Jin-Hee_Lee.jpg&quot;],&quot;location&quot;:[0,null],&quot;website&quot;:[0,null],&quot;twitter&quot;:[0,null],&quot;facebook&quot;:[0,null],&quot;publiclyIndex&quot;:[0,true]}]]],&quot;meta_description&quot;:[0,&quot;Blocking bots isnГўВҖВҷt enough anymore. props="{&quot;post&quot;:[0,{&quot;id&quot;:[0,&quot;3oZLDQYiufcZZYvGXwxpKd&quot;],&quot;title&quot;:[0,&quot;Announcing Cloudflare Account Abuse Protection: prevent fraudulent attacks from bots and humans&quot;],&quot;slug&quot;:[0,&quot;account-abuse-protection&quot;],&quot;excerpt&quot;:[0,&quot;Blocking bots isnГўВҖВҷt enough anymore. CloudflareГўВҖВҷs new fraud prevention capabilities ГўВҖВ” now available in Early Access ГўВҖВ” help stop account abuse before it starts.&quot;],&quot;featured&quot;:[0,false],&quot;html&quot;:[0,&quot;&lt;p&gt;Today, Cloudflare is introducing a new suite of fraud prevention capabilities designed to stop account abuse before it starts. We&amp;#39;ve spent years empowering Cloudflare customers to protect their applications from automated attacks, but the threat landscape has evolved. The industrialization of hybrid automated-and-human abuse presents a complex security challenge to website owners. Consider, for instance, a single account thatГўВҖВҷs accessed from New York, London, and San Francisco in the same five minutes. The core question in this case is not ГўВҖВңIs this automated?ГўВҖВқ but rather ГўВҖВңIs this authentic?ГўВҖВқГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Website owners need the tools to stop abuse on their website, no matter who itГўВҖВҷs coming from&lt;/b&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;During our Birthday Week in 2024, we gifted &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/detections/leaked-credentials/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;leaked credentials detection&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; to all customers, including everyone on a Free plan. Since then, we&amp;#39;ve added &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/bots/additional-configurations/detection-ids/#account-takeover-detections\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;account takeover detection IDs&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; as part of our &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/application-services/products/bot-management/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;bot management solution&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; to help identify bots attacking your login pages.ГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Now, weГўВҖВҷre combining these powerful tools with new ones. &lt;b&gt;Disposable email check&lt;/b&gt; and &lt;b&gt;email risk &lt;/b&gt;help you enforce security preferences for users who sign up with throwaway email addresses, a common tactic for fake account creation and promotion abuse, or whose emails are deemed risky based on email patterns and infrastructure. WeГўВҖВҷre also thrilled to introduce &lt;b&gt;Hashed User IDs&lt;/b&gt; ГўВҖВ” per-domain identifiers generated by cryptographically hashing usernames ГўВҖВ” that give customers better insight into suspicious account activity and greater ability to mitigate potentially fraudulent traffic, without compromising end user privacy.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;The new capabilities weГўВҖВҷre announcing today go beyond automation, identifying abusive behavior and risky identities among human users &lt;/b&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;i&gt;and&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;b&gt; bots. &lt;/b&gt;&lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/bots/account-abuse-protection/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Account Abuse Protection&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; is available in Early Access, and any Bot Management Enterprise customer can use these features at no additional cost for a limited period, until the general availability of Cloudflare Fraud Prevention later this year. If you want to learn more about this Early Access capability, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/lp/account-abuse-protection/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;sign up here&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h3 id=\&quot;leaked-credentials-make-logins-all-too-vulnerable\&quot;&gt;Leaked credentials make logins all too vulnerable&lt;/h3&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#leaked-credentials-make-logins-all-too-vulnerable\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;The barrier to entry for fraudulent behavior is dangerously low, especially with the availability of massive datasets and access to automated tools that commit account fraud at scale. Website owners arenГўВҖВҷt just dealing with individual hackers, but industrialized fraud. Last year, we highlighted how &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/password-reuse-rampant-half-user-logins-compromised/\&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;41% of logins across our network use leaked credentials&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. This number has only grown following the exposure of a database holding &lt;a href=\&quot;https://cybernews.com/security/billions-credentials-exposed-infostealers-data-leak/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;16 billion records&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, and multiple high-profile breaches have since come to light.ГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;WhatГўВҖВҷs more, users reuse passwords across multiple platforms, meaning a single leak from years ago can still unlock a high-value retail or even a bank account today. Our &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/detections/leaked-credentials/#leaked-credentials-fields\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;leaked credential check&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; is a free feature that checks whether a password has been leaked in a known data breach of another service or application on the Internet. This is a privacy-preserving credential checking service that helps protect our users from compromised credentials, meaning Cloudflare performs these checks without accessing or storing plaintext end user passwords. &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/helping-keep-customers-safe-with-leaked-password-notification/#how-does-cloudflare-check-for-leaked-credentials\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Passwords are hashed ГўВҖВ” i.e., converted into a random string of characters using a cryptographic algorithm ГўВҖВ” for the purpose of comparing them against a database of leaked credentials.&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; If you havenГўВҖВҷt already turned on our &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/detections/leaked-credentials/#leaked-credentials-fields\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;leaked credential check&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, enable it now to keep your accounts safe from easy hacks!&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Access to a large database of leaked credentials is only useful if an attacker can cycle through them quickly across many sites to identify which accounts are still vulnerable due to password reuse. In our Black Friday analysis in 2024, we observed that more than &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/grinch-bot-2024/\&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;60% of traffic to login pages across our network was automated&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. ThatГўВҖВҷs a lot of bots trying to break in.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;To help customers protect their login endpoints from constant bombardment, we added &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/learning/access-management/account-takeover/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;account takeover&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/bots/additional-configurations/detection-ids/account-takeover-detections/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;(ATO)-specific detections&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; to highlight suspicious traffic patterns. This is part of our recent focus on &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/per-customer-bot-defenses/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;per-customer detections&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, in which we provide behavioral anomaly detection unique to each bot management customer. Today, bot management customers can see and mitigate attempted ATO attacks in their login requests directly on the Security analytics dashboard.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/3f2nQ5wBVQ2WqiKGsjVWJe/3c1011ced84e46f65938f32c88035de9/image5.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1334\&quot; height=\&quot;492\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;In the card on the left within the Security analytics dashboard, you can view and address attempted account takeover attacks.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;In the last week, our ATO detections combined caught an average of &lt;b&gt;6.9 billion suspicious login attempts&lt;/b&gt; daily, across our network. These ATO detections, along with the many other detection mechanisms in our bot management solution, create a &lt;i&gt;layered defense&lt;/i&gt; against ATO and other malicious automated attacks.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h3 id=\&quot;from-automation-to-intent-and-identity\&quot;&gt;From automation to intent and identity&lt;/h3&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#from-automation-to-intent-and-identity\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;To discern automation, or to discern intent and identity? That is the question. Our answer: yes and yes, as both are critical layers of a robust security posture. Attackers now operate at a scale previously reserved for enterprise services: they leverage massive credential leaks, use human-powered fraud farms to spoof devices and locations, and create synthetic identities to maintain thousands ГўВҖВ” even millions ГўВҖВ” of fake accounts for promotion and platform abuse. A human being with automated tools could be draining accounts, abusing promotions, committing payment fraud, or all of the above.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Beyond that, automation is accessible like never before, particularly as users become better acquainted with using &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/learning/ai/what-is-agentic-ai/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;AI agents&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; and even long-standing, ГўВҖВңtraditionalГўВҖВқ browsers move toward having agentic capabilities by default. Whether itГўВҖВҷs a lone actor using an AI agent or a coordinated fraud campaign, the threat isnГўВҖВҷt as simple as a single script ГўВҖВ” it can involve human intent, with automated execution.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Consider the following scenarios weГўВҖВҷve heard from our customers:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;We have 1,000 new users this month, but more than half of them are fake identities who benefit from a free trial, then disappear.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;The attacker logged in with the correct password, so how do I know that it isnГўВҖВҷt the real user?&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;This entity is acting at human pace, and they are draining accounts.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;These problems can&amp;#39;t be solved by &lt;i&gt;only&lt;/i&gt; assessing automation; they require checking for authenticity and integrity. This is the gap that our dedicated fraud prevention capabilities address.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h3 id=\&quot;assessing-suspicious-emails\&quot;&gt;Assessing suspicious emails&lt;/h3&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#assessing-suspicious-emails\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;LetГўВҖВҷs start by assessing the earliest point of potential account abuse: account creation. Fake or bulk account creation is one of the biggest topics in conversations about website fraud, as it can open the door for attackers to access an application ГўВҖВ” or even an entire business model.ГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Cloudflare is giving customers the tools to assess suspicious account creation at the source in two ways:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Disposable email check&lt;/b&gt;: Detect when users sign up with disposable, or throwaway, email addresses commonly used for promotion abuse and fake account creation. These disposable email services allow attackers to spin up thousands of &amp;quot;unique&amp;quot; accounts without maintaining real infrastructure, particularly unauthenticated disposable emails that provide instant access without account creation or free unlimited email aliases. Customers can use this binary field as they build rules to enforce security preferences, choosing to block all disposable emails outright, or perhaps issuing a &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/cloudflare-challenges/challenge-types/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;challenge&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; to anyone attempting to create an account with a disposable email.\n&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/3PQC7PqKWrhl5c4OCXu5Ha/9340e3b49cc396ca5f5d01d34fd529d5/image2.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1638\&quot; height=\&quot;344\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Email risk:&lt;/b&gt; Cloudflare analyzes email patterns and infrastructure to provide risk tiers (low, medium, high) that customers can use in security rules. We know that not all email addresses are created equal; an address with the format &lt;code&gt;firstname.lastname@knowndomain.com&lt;/code&gt; carries different risk characteristics than &lt;code&gt;xk7q9m2p@newdomain.xyz&lt;/code&gt;. Email risk tiers allow customers to express their tolerance for risk and friction at the point of account creation.ГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;p&gt;Both disposable email check and email risk are now available in security analytics and security rules, equipping website owners to protect their account creation flow. These detections address a fundamental problem: by the time an account is committing abuse, it&amp;#39;s already too late. The website owner has already paid acquisition costs, the fraudulent user has consumed promotional credits, and remediation requires manual review. Mitigating suspicious emails means adding the appropriate friction at signup ГўВҖВ” the moment it matters most.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h3 id=\&quot;introducing-hashed-user-ids\&quot;&gt;Introducing Hashed User IDs&lt;/h3&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#introducing-hashed-user-ids\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;Understanding patterns of abuse requires &lt;i&gt;visibility&lt;/i&gt;: not only into the network, but of account activity. Traditionally, security has meant looking through the lens of IPs and isolated HTTP requests to spot automated activity, but website owners arenГўВҖВҷt just thinking in terms of network signals; they are also considering their users and known accounts. ThatГўВҖВҷs why weГўВҖВҷre expanding our mitigation toolbox to match the way applications are actually structured, focusing on user-based detection of fraudulent activity.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Attackers can effortlessly rotate IPs to hide their tracks. But forcing them to repeatedly generate new, credible accounts introduces massive friction, especially when combined with account creation protections. When we look past the network layer and map fraudulent actions to a given compromised or abusive account, we can spot targeted behavior tied to a single, persistent actor and put a stop to the abuse. In this way, weГўВҖВҷre shifting the defense strategy to the account level, instead of playing whack-a-mole with rotating IP addresses and residential proxies. This means that &lt;b&gt;our customers can mitigate abusive behavior based on the way &lt;/b&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;i&gt;their&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;b&gt; applications separate identity&lt;/b&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;To arm website owners with this capability, Cloudflare is releasing a &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/bots/account-abuse-protection/#user-id\&quot;&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;u&gt;Hashed User ID&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/a&gt; that customers can use in &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/analytics/security-analytics/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Security analytics&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/custom-rules/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Security rules&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, and &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/rules/transform/managed-transforms/reference/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Managed Transforms&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. User IDs are per-domain, cryptographically hashed versions of the values in the username field, and each user ID is an encrypted, unique, and stable identifier generated for a given username on a customer application. &lt;b&gt;Importantly, the actual username is not logged or stored by Cloudflare as part of this service.&lt;/b&gt; As with leaked credentials check and ATO detections, which identify login traffic and then encrypt credentials for comparison, we are prioritizing end user privacy while empowering our customers to take action against fraudulent behavior.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;With access to Hashed User IDs, website owners can:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;See top users: Which accounts have the most activity?&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;See when a unique user logs in from a country they usually donГўВҖВҷt ГўВҖВ” or multiple countries in one day!&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;Mitigate traffic based on unique user, such as blocking a user with historically suspicious activity.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;Combine fields to see when accounts are being targeted with leaked credentials.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;See what network patterns or signals are associated with unique users.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/3f7Jm4HnngjYEmKG8QSiyC/2ae3543f0cd0eb072a0c4c2bb12c4436/image4.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1110\&quot; height=\&quot;736\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;The expanded view of a single Hashed User ID within the Security analytics dashboard, showing the activity details of that unique user, including their login location and their browser.ГӮВ &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;This user-level visibility transforms how website owners can investigate and mitigate traffic. Instead of examining individual requests in isolation, our customers can see the full picture of how attackers are targeting and hiding among legitimate users.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h3 id=\&quot;take-the-next-step-in-account-protection-today\&quot;&gt;Take the next step in account protection today&lt;/h3&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#take-the-next-step-in-account-protection-today\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;If you want to learn more about this Early Access capability, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/lp/account-abuse-protection/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;sign up here&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. All Bot Management Enterprise customers are eligible to add these new Account Abuse Protection features today, and weГўВҖВҷd love to open the conversation with any and all &lt;a href=\&quot;http://www.cloudflare.com/lp/account-abuse-protection\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;prospective Bot Management customers&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;While bot detections will continue to answer the question of automation and intent, fraud detections delve into the question of authenticity. Together, they give website owners comprehensive tools to fight against the full spectrum of account abuse. This suite is one step in our ongoing investment to protect the entire user journey ГўВҖВ” from account creation and login to secure checkouts and the integrity of every interaction.&lt;/p&gt;&quot;],&quot;published_at&quot;:[0,&quot;2026-03-12T13:00+08:00&quot;],&quot;updated_at&quot;:[0,&quot;2026-03-12T13:00:12.058Z&quot;],&quot;feature_image&quot;:[0,&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/1xUHwg1io7QsO9sswX7GpD/2066c94abed41c9b6e4397173955cae7/image3.png&quot;],&quot;tags&quot;:[1,[[0,{&quot;id&quot;:[0,&quot;5tL3rXMWKG616Xmbnao9Oh&quot;],&quot;name&quot;:[0,&quot;Fraud&quot;],&quot;slug&quot;:[0,&quot;fraud&quot;]}],[0,{&quot;id&quot;:[0,&quot;6Mp7ouACN2rT3YjL1xaXJx&quot;],&quot;name&quot;:[0,&quot;Security&quot;],&quot;slug&quot;:[0,&quot;security&quot;]}]]],&quot;relatedTags&quot;:[0],&quot;authors&quot;:[1,[[0,{&quot;name&quot;:[0,&quot;Jin-Hee Lee&quot;],&quot;slug&quot;:[0,&quot;jin-hee-lee&quot;],&quot;bio&quot;:[0,null],&quot;profile_image&quot;:[0,&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/47LTVC3FaSVzkAumTWfFIi/4424dfc2819cbc4a8fff6b72ce93047e/Jin-Hee_Lee.jpg&quot;],&quot;location&quot;:[0,null],&quot;website&quot;:[0,null],&quot;twitter&quot;:[0,null],&quot;facebook&quot;:[0,null],&quot;publiclyIndex&quot;:[0,true]}]]],&quot;meta_description&quot;:[0,&quot;Blocking bots isnГўВҖВҷt enough anymore. We are also making AI discovery free for all plans, to help teams find and secure shadow AI deployments.&quot;],&quot;featured&quot;:[0,false],&quot;html&quot;:[0,&quot;&lt;p&gt;CloudflareГўВҖВҷs &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/demos/protect-ai-apps/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;AI Security for Apps&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; detects and mitigates threats to AI-powered applications. Today, we&amp;#39;re announcing that it is generally available.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;WeГўВҖВҷre shipping with new capabilities like detection for custom topics, and we&amp;#39;re making AI endpoint discovery free for every Cloudflare customerГўВҖВ”including those on Free, Pro, and Business plansГўВҖВ”to give everyone visibility into where AI is deployed across their Internet-facing apps.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;We&amp;#39;re also announcing an expanded collaboration with IBM, which has chosen Cloudflare to deliver AI security to its cloud customers. And weГўВҖВҷre partnering with Wiz to give mutual customers a unified view of their AI security posture.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h2 id=\&quot;a-new-kind-of-attack-surface\&quot;&gt;A new kind of attack surface&lt;/h2&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#a-new-kind-of-attack-surface\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;Traditional web applications have defined operations: check a bank balance, make a transfer. You can write deterministic rules to secure those interactions.ГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;AI-powered applications and agents are different. They accept natural language and generate unpredictable responses. There&amp;#39;s no fixed set of operations to allow or deny, because the inputs and outputs are probabilistic. Attackers can manipulate large language models to take unauthorized actions or leak sensitive data. Prompt injection, sensitive information disclosure, and unbounded consumption are just a few of the risks cataloged in the &lt;a href=\&quot;https://genai.owasp.org/llm-top-10/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;OWASP Top 10 for LLM Applications&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;These risks escalate as AI applications become agents. When an AI gains access to tool callsГўВҖВ”processing refunds, modifying accounts, providing discounts, or accessing customer dataГўВҖВ”a single malicious prompt becomes an immediate security incident.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Customers tell us what theyГўВҖВҷre up against. &amp;quot;Most of Newfold Digital&amp;#39;s teams are putting in their own Generative AI safeguards, but everybody is innovating so quickly that there are inevitably going to be some gaps eventually,ГўВҖВқ says Rick Radinger, Principal Systems Architect at Newfold Digital, which operates Bluehost, HostGator, and Domain.com. &lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h2 id=\&quot;what-ai-security-for-apps-does\&quot;&gt;What AI Security for Apps does&lt;/h2&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#what-ai-security-for-apps-does\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;We built AI Security for Apps to address this. It sits in front of your AI-powered applications, whether you&amp;#39;re using a third-party model or hosting your own, as part of Cloudflare&amp;#39;s &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.cloudflare.com/learning/cdn/glossary/reverse-proxy/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;reverse proxy&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. It helps you (1) discover AI-powered apps across your web property, (2) detect malicious or off-policy behavior to those endpoints, and (3) mitigate threats via the familiar WAF rule builder. &lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/5xpmckBUupzELjYOSx5bAF/cace1ab2ed2dd54d8d7a7ff60587ef65/BLOG-3128_2.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;BLOG-3128 2\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1999\&quot; height=\&quot;650\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h3 id=\&quot;discovery-now-free-for-everyone\&quot;&gt;Discovery ГўВҖВ” now free for everyone&lt;/h3&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#discovery-now-free-for-everyone\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;Before you can protect your LLM-powered applications, you need to know where they&amp;#39;re being used. We often hear from security teams who donГўВҖВҷt have a complete picture of AI deployments across their apps, especially as the LLM market evolves and developers swap out models and providers.ГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;AI Security for Apps automatically identifies LLM-powered endpoints across your web properties, regardless of where theyГўВҖВҷre hosted or what the model is. Starting today, this capability is free for every Cloudflare customer, including Free, Pro, and Business plans.ГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/2dBKhU5VNbzAePDAnaHkTK/3f6a569e495e03c3e2afca4d6183e02d/image4.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;BLOG-3128 3\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1999\&quot; height=\&quot;1000\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;CloudflareГўВҖВҷs dashboard page of web assets, showing 2 example endpoints labelled as &lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;code&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;cf-llm&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Discovering these endpoints automatically requires more than matching common path patterns like &lt;code&gt;/chat/completions&lt;/code&gt;. Many AI-powered applications don&amp;#39;t have a chat interface: think product search, property valuation tools, or recommendation engines. We built a &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/take-control-of-public-ai-application-security-with-cloudflare-firewall-for-ai/#discovering-llm-powered-applications\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;detection system that looks at how endpoints behave&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, not what they&amp;#39;re called. To confidently identify AI-powered endpoints, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/api-shield/security/api-discovery/#requirements\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;sufficient valid traffic&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; is required.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;AI-powered endpoints that have been discovered will be visible under &lt;a href=\&quot;https://dash.cloudflare.com/?to=/:account/:zone/security/web-assets\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Security ГўВҶВ’ Web Assets&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, labeled as &lt;code&gt;cf-llm&lt;/code&gt;. For customers on a Free plan, endpoint discovery is initiated when you first navigate to the &lt;a href=\&quot;https://dash.cloudflare.com/?to=/:account/:zone/security/web-assets/discovery\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Discovery page&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. For customers on a paid plan, discovery occurs automatically in the background on a recurring basis. If your AI-powered endpoints have been discovered, you can review them immediately.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h3 id=\&quot;detection\&quot;&gt;Detection&lt;/h3&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#detection\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;AI Security for Apps detections follow the &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/waf/detections/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;always-on approach&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; for traffic to your AI-powered endpoints. Each prompt is run through multiple detection modules for prompt injection, PII exposure, and sensitive or toxic topics. The resultsГўВҖВ”whether the prompt was malicious or notГўВҖВ”are attached as metadata you can use in custom WAF rules to enforce your policies. We are continuously exploring ways to leverage our global network, which sees traffic from roughly &lt;a href=\&quot;https://w3techs.com/technologies/history_overview/proxy/all\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;20% of the web&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, to identify new attack patterns across millions of sites before they reach yours.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/7oGjcaUL5L9zlAkz8lSmXv/4354a9555135e19de5c93d3d113e6790/BLOG-3128_4.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;BLOG-3128 4\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1922\&quot; height=\&quot;444\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h4 id=\&quot;new-in-ga-custom-topics-detection\&quot;&gt;New in GA: Custom topics detection&lt;/h4&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#new-in-ga-custom-topics-detection\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;The product ships with built-in detection for common threats: prompt injections, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/take-control-of-public-ai-application-security-with-cloudflare-firewall-for-ai/#detecting-prompts-designed-to-leak-pii\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;PII extraction&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, and &lt;a href=\&quot;https://blog.cloudflare.com/block-unsafe-llm-prompts-with-firewall-for-ai/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;toxic topics&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. But every business has its own definition of what&amp;#39;s off-limits. A financial services company might need to detect discussions of specific securities. A healthcare company might need to flag conversations that touch on patient data. A retailer might want to know when customers are asking about competitor products.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The new custom topics feature lets you define these categories. You specify the topic, we inspect the prompt and output a relevance score that you can use to log, block, or handle however you decide. Our goal is to build an extensible tool that flexes to your use cases.&lt;/p&gt;\n          &lt;figure class=\&quot;kg-card kg-image-card\&quot;&gt;\n          &lt;Image src=\&quot;https://cf-assets.www.cloudflare.com/zkvhlag99gkb/1WzPhy11ZmUXDGZjft4sY1/7ebfafaf2114eaba83a829694837fc2c/image1.png\&quot; alt=\&quot;BLOG-3128 5\&quot; class=\&quot;kg-image\&quot; width=\&quot;1946\&quot; height=\&quot;819\&quot; loading=\&quot;lazy\&quot;/&gt;\n          &lt;/figure&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;sup&gt;&lt;i&gt;Prompt relevance score inside of AI Security for Apps&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h4 id=\&quot;new-in-ga-custom-prompt-extraction\&quot;&gt;New in GA: Custom prompt extraction&lt;/h4&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#new-in-ga-custom-prompt-extraction\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;AI Security for Apps enforces guardrails before unsafe prompts can reach your infrastructure. To run detections accurately and provide real-time protection, we first need to identify the prompt within the request payload. Prompts can live anywhere in a request body, and different LLM providers structure their APIs differently. OpenAI and most providers use &lt;code&gt;$.messages[*].content&lt;/code&gt; for chat completions. Anthropic&amp;#39;s batch API nests prompts inside &lt;code&gt;$.requests[*].params.messages[*].content&lt;/code&gt;. Your custom property valuation tool might use &lt;code&gt;$.property_description&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Out of the box, we support the standard formats used by OpenAI, Anthropic, Google Gemini, Mistral, Cohere, xAI, DeepSeek, and others. When we can&amp;#39;t match a known pattern, we apply a default-secure posture and run detection on the entire request body. This can introduce false positives when the payload contains fields that are sensitive but don&amp;#39;t feed directly to an AI model, for example, a &lt;code&gt;$.customer_name&lt;/code&gt; field alongside the actual prompt might trigger PII detection unnecessarily.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Soon, you&amp;#39;ll be able to define your own JSONPath expressions to tell us exactly where to find the prompt. This will reduce false positives and lead to more accurate detections. We&amp;#39;re also building a prompt-learning capability that will automatically adapt to your application&amp;#39;s structure over time.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h3 id=\&quot;mitigation\&quot;&gt;Mitigation&lt;/h3&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#mitigation\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;Once a threat is identified and scored, you can block it, log it, or deliver custom responses, using the same WAF rules engine you already use for the rest of your application security. The power of CloudflareГўВҖВҷs shared platform is that you can combine AI-specific signals with everything else we know about a request, represented by &lt;a href=\&quot;https://developers.cloudflare.com/ruleset-engine/rules-language/fields/reference/\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;hundreds of fields&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt; available in the WAF. A prompt injection attempt is suspicious. A prompt injection attempt from an IP thatГўВҖВҷs been probing your login page, using a browser fingerprint associated with previous attacks, and rotating through a botnet is a different story. Point solutions that only see the AI layer canГўВҖВҷt make these connections.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;This unified security layer is exactly what they need at Newfold Digital to discover, label, and protect AI endpoints, says Radinger: ГўВҖВңWe look forward to using it across all these projects to serve as a fail-safe.&amp;quot;&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h2 id=\&quot;growing-ecosystem\&quot;&gt;Growing ecosystem&lt;/h2&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#growing-ecosystem\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;AI Security for Applications will also be available through Cloudflare&amp;#39;s growing ecosystem, including through integration with IBM Cloud. Through &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.ibm.com/products/cloud-internet-services\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;IBM Cloud Internet Services (CIS)&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, end users can already procure advanced application security solutions and manage them directly through their IBM Cloud account.ГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;We&amp;#39;re also partnering with Wiz to connect AI Security for Applications with &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.wiz.io/solutions/ai-spm\&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;Wiz AI Security&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, giving mutual customers a unified view of their AI security posture, from model and agent discovery in the cloud to application-layer guardrails at the edge.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h2 id=\&quot;how-to-get-started\&quot;&gt;How to get started&lt;/h2&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#how-to-get-started\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;AI Security for Apps is available now for CloudflareГўВҖВҷs Enterprise customers. Log Explorer supports 14 additional Cloudflare datasets, enabling users to have a 360-degree view of their network.&quot;],&quot;featured&quot;:[0,false],&quot;html&quot;:[0,&quot;&lt;p&gt;In the world of cybersecurity, a single data point is rarely the whole story. Modern attackers donГўВҖВҷt just knock on the front door; they probe your APIs, flood your network with &amp;quot;noise&amp;quot; to distract your team, and attempt to slide through applications and servers using stolen credentials.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;To stop these multi-vector attacks, you need the full picture. By using Cloudflare Log Explorer to conduct security forensics, you get 360-degree visibility through the integration of 14 new datasets, covering the full surface of CloudflareГўВҖВҷs Application Services and Cloudflare One product portfolios. By correlating telemetry from application-layer HTTP requests, network-layer DDoS and Firewall logs, and Zero Trust Access events, security analysts can significantly reduce Mean Time to Detect (MTTD) and effectively unmask sophisticated, multi-layered attacks.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Read on to learn more about how Log Explorer gives security teams the ultimate landscape for rapid, deep-dive forensics.&lt;/p&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h2 id=\&quot;the-flight-recorder-for-your-entire-stack\&quot;&gt;The flight recorder for your entire stack&lt;/h2&gt;\n      &lt;a href=\&quot;#the-flight-recorder-for-your-entire-stack\&quot; aria-hidden=\&quot;true\&quot; class=\&quot;relative sm:absolute sm:-start-5\&quot;&gt;\n        &lt;svg width=\&quot;16\&quot; height=\&quot;16\&quot; viewBox=\&quot;0 0 24 24\&quot;&gt;&lt;path fill=\&quot;currentcolor\&quot; d=\&quot;m12.11 15.39-3.88 3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1-3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0-3.5l3.88-3.88a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-3.88 3.89a4.48 4.48 0 0 0 6.33 6.33l3.89-3.88a1 1 0 1 0-1.42-1.42Zm8.58-12.08a4.49 4.49 0 0 0-6.33 0l-3.89 3.88a1 1 0 0 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.88a2.52 2.52 0 0 1 3.5 0 2.47 2.47 0 0 1 0 3.5l-3.88 3.88a1 1 0 1 0 1.42 1.42l3.88-3.89a4.49 4.49 0 0 0 0-6.33ZM8.83 15.17a1 1 0 0 0 1.1.22 1 1 0 0 0 .32-.22l4.92-4.92a1 1 0 0 0-1.42-1.42l-4.92 4.92a1 1 0 0 0 0 1.42Z\&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\n      &lt;/a&gt;\n    &lt;/div&gt;\n    &lt;p&gt;The contemporary digital landscape requires deep, correlated telemetry to defend against adversaries using multiple attack vectors. Raw logs serve as the &amp;quot;flight recorder&amp;quot; for an application, capturing every single interaction, attack attempt, and performance bottleneck. And because Cloudflare sits at the edge, between your users and your servers, all of these events are logged before the requests even reach your infrastructure.ГӮВ &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Cloudflare Log performance.&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;table&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;HTTP Requests&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;As the most comprehensive dataset, it serves as the &amp;quot;primary record&amp;quot; of all application-layer traffic, enabling the reconstruction of session activity, exploit attempts, and bot patterns.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Firewall Events&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;Provides critical evidence of blocked or challenged threats, allowing analysts to identify the specific WAF rules, IP reputations, or custom filters that intercepted an attack.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;DNS Logs&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;Identify cache poisoning attempts, domain hijacking, and infrastructure-level reconnaissance by tracking every query resolved at the authoritative edge.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;NEL (Network Error Logging) Reports&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;Distinguish between a coordinated Layer 7 DDoS attack and legitimate network connectivity issues by tracking client-side browser errors.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Spectrum Events&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;For non-web applications, these logs provide visibility into L4 traffic (TCP/UDP), helping to identify anomalies or brute-force attacks against protocols like SSH, RDP, or custom gaming traffic.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Page Shield&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;Track and audit unauthorized changes to your site&amp;#39;s client-side environment such as JavaScript, outbound connections.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Zaraz unauthorized script behaviors.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/table&gt;\n    &lt;div class=\&quot;flex anchor relative\&quot;&gt;\n      &lt;h4
